# NanoAOD production campaign for 2018UL NMSSM X &rightarrow; YH &rightarrow; bb&tau;&tau; samples

## Used configuration and setup:

* conditions: [`configuration/conditions.yaml`](../configuration/conditions.yaml)
* cmsdriver settings for nanoAOD: [`configuration/cmsdriver_nanoaod_specifics.yaml`](../configuration/cmsdriver_nanoaod_specifics.yaml)
* datasets: [`configuration/datasets_miniaod_nmssm_2018UL.yaml`](../configuration/datasets_miniaod_nmssm_2018UL.yaml)
* crab config template: [`crab_configuration/crab_template.py`](../crab_configuration/crab_template.py)
* CMSSW release: CMSSW_13_0_21
* `CMSSWWithCrab` commit: [`768f0ef`](https://github.com/KIT-CMS/CMSSWWithCrab/tree/768f0efda7f0ee34409309acd1e3c957b479320f)

## Creation of CMSSW and Crab configs call

General call:

```bash
./create_configs.py --work-directory /eos/user/$(whoami | head -c 1)/$(whoami)/nanoaodv12_production/ \
                                  --datasets configuration/datasets_miniaod_nmssm_2018UL.yaml \
                                  --conditions configuration/conditions.yaml \
                                  --cmsdriver configuration/cmsdriver_nanoaod_specifics.yaml \
                                  --nThreads 4 --numCores 4 --maxMemoryMBperCore 750 --maxJobRuntimeMin 1440 \
                                  --publication --splitting EventAwareLumiBased --unitsPerJob 500000 --siteWhitelist T1_DE_KIT
```

### Adaptations during production campaign

Some jobs needed resubmission with longer maximum runtime, `FileBased` splitting, and more granular settings for the units per job.

## Managing of crab tasks call

Initial calls will be presented in the following, which can be adapted further for resubmission supplemented with available resubmission options (see `./create_configs.py --help`).

```bash
./crab_manager.py --crab-config-pattern /eos/$(whoami | head -c 1)/$(whoami)/nanoaodv12_production/crabconfigs/*.py
```

The datasets corresponding to the following DAS keys have resulted from failed productions, so **do not use them**:

- `/NMSSM_XToYHTo2B2Tau_MX-600_MY-100_TuneCP5_13TeV-madgraph-pythia8/momolch-mc_2018UL_nmssm_2b2tau_NMSSM_XToYHTo2B2Tau_MX-600_MY-100_1740493271-00000000000000000000000000000000/USER`
- `/NMSSM_XToYHTo2B2Tau_MX-3000_MY-1800_TuneCP5_13TeV-madgraph-pythia8/momolch-mc_2018UL_nmssm_2b2tau_NMSSM_XToYHTo2B2Tau_MX-3000_MY-1800_1740493271-00000000000000000000000000000000/USER`
- `/NMSSM_XToYHTo2B2Tau_MX-3000_MY-1800_TuneCP5_13TeV-madgraph-pythia8/momolch-mc_2018UL_nmssm_2b2tau_NMSSM_XToYHTo2B2Tau_MX-3000_MY-1800_1741082633-00000000000000000000000000000000/USER`

## Results

The finished production campaign can be seen at CMS Grafana:

https://monit-grafana.cern.ch/goto/4jRchkoHg?orgId=11

The resulting datasets, without outputs of failed tasks, are (accessible via DAS webpage or `dasgoclient`, using `prod/phys03` DBS instance):
